   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">1998 Davis Cup World Group</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> 
    <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> 
    <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: 
       <a href="/wiki/1998_Davis_Cup" title="1998 Davis Cup">1998 Davis Cup</a>
      </div> 
      <p>The <b>World Group</b> was the highest level of <a href="/wiki/Davis_Cup" title="Davis Cup">Davis Cup</a> competition in 1998. The first-round losers went into the <a href="/w/index.php?title=1998_Davis_Cup_World_Group_Play-offs&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="1998 Davis Cup World Group Play-offs (page does not exist)">Davis Cup World Group Play-offs</a>, and the winners progress to the quarterfinals. The quarterfinalists were guaranteed a World Group spot for 1999. </p> 
      <div id="toc" class="toc">

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Brazil_vs._Spain">Brazil vs. Spain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998_Davis_Cup_World_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Brazil vs. Spain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <table cellpadding="3" cellspacing="0" style="background: #f9f9f9; border: 1px #aaa solid; font-size: 95%; float: none; width: 70%"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
